I like this place. The employees are very nice & helpful. If there's something you can't find they will go out of their way to help you. The store is well-stocked & organized & they carry supplies for all different kinds of critters. They even have an area where you can wash your pets if you don't want to do that in your home. I feel some of the items are a little pricey however they're not out of range of a lot of other places. They also don't  hassle you about returns. Or at least I haven't encountered that. One thing I don't like is that they close at 8 p.m. instead of 9 p.m. like the other chain pet supply stores, but, that's just a minor thing. I recommend this place to anyone who is thinking about stopping here or needs a go to place for your pet supply needs.< /review>
